### èµ·é£(èµ·é£›) â†’ é£›(é£›)
- **definition:** fly; flutter; hover; rush
- **pinyin:** fÄ“i
- **components:**
  - å‡
    - shÄ“ng
    - rise
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a bird flying upwards, resembles a tasseled å‡(å‡) (shÄ“ng, "rise")
  - **interpretation:** The character é£›(fÄ“i, "fly") is a pictogram representing a bird in flight, capturing the upward motion and dynamic nature of flying. Its resemblance to å‡(å‡) reflects the concept of rising or ascending, which is inherent to the action of flying.
